### [1] [Visons in Kitaev Spin Liquids with Majorana Fermi Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23014)
*Caio V. S. Soares,Rodrigo G. Pereira*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究Kitaev量子自旋液体中vison激发与Majorana费米子费米面的相互作用，发现费米面增大会导致vison能隙减小，暗示量子自旋液体基态的不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究当Kitaev模型中Majorana费米子形成费米面时，vison激发的性质及其对量子自旋液体基态稳定性的影响。

Method: 对比有限格点上的数值计算与基于格林函数技术的解析方法，分析vison能隙随费米面大小的变化，以及Majorana-vison散射势对局域自旋关联的调制。

Result: 发现vison能隙随费米面增大而减小，表明量子自旋液体基态存在不稳定性；同时较大的费米面会抑制Majorana-vison散射势引起的局域自旋关联变化。

Conclusion: Kitaev量子自旋液体中费米面的存在会 destabilize 基态，vison能隙的减小是这一不稳定性的信号。

Abstract: The excitation spectrum of Kitaev quantum spin liquids consists of itinerant Majorana fermions, which can be gapless or gapped, and vortices of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge field, known as visons, which are always gapped. In this work, we investigate visons in Kitaev-type models where the Majorana fermions form a Fermi surface. In this case, the creation of a vison pair is analogous to introducing a local impurity potential in a metal. Since the gapless modes lead to strong finite-size effects, we compare the numerical calculation of the vison gap on finite lattices with the result from an analytical approach based on Green's function techniques. We find that the vison gap decreases as the size of the Fermi surface increases, signalling an instability of the quantum spin liquid ground state. We also show that larger Fermi surfaces tend to suppress the change in local spin correlations due to the Majorana-vison scattering potential.

</details>


### [2] [Exact momentum-space analysis of small spin-1/2 $J_1$-$J_2$ rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23149)
*Zimeng Li,Ning Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了N=6和8的自旋1/2 J1-J2环，利用精确的少磁子布洛赫态实现了哈密顿量的块对角化（最多四维），部分解析求解了本征态。对于六位点各向异性环，发现了一类同时是哈密顿量和总角动量算符本征态的子集（尽管后者不守恒）。对于各向同性环，实现了多个重要态（包括Majumdar-Ghosh基态和Hamada-Kane-Nakagawa-Natsume基态）的动量空间表示，明确证明了N=6时这些态与实空间表示的等价性。HKNN基态的结构表明，对于任意偶数N，该态可能表现为N/2个连续下自旋束缚的"束缚态"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 求解小尺寸自旋1/2 J1-J2环（N=6和8）的精确本征态，揭示各向异性与各向同性情形下的量子态结构，特别是理解著名的Majumdar-Ghosh基态和Hamada-Kane-Nakagawa-Natsume基态在动量空间的表现形式及其物理本质。

Method: 利用精确的少磁子布洛赫态构造块对角化哈密顿量（最大块矩阵维度为四维），通过解析方法求解部分本征态，并在各向同性和各向异性情形下分析本征态的对称性性质。

Result: 1) 实现了哈密顿量的块对角化，最大块矩阵维度仅为四维；2) 在六位点各向异性环中发现了一类特殊的本征态，同时是哈密顿量和非守恒的总角动量算符的本征态；3) 在N=6和8的各向同性环中，给出了MG基态和HKNN基态等重要态的动量空间表示；4) 明确证明了N=6时动量空间态与实空间态的等价性；5) 揭示了HKNN基态可能对应于N/2个连续下自旋的束缚态结构。

Conclusion: 少磁子布洛赫态方法能有效简化小尺寸自旋环的求解。HKNN基态在任意偶数N下可能表现为N/2个连续下自旋的束缚态，这为理解更大尺寸J1-J2系统中的量子态结构提供了重要线索。

Abstract: This paper considers an $N$-site spin-1/2 $J_1$-$J_2$ ring with $N=6$ and $8$. With the help of a set of exact few-magnon Bloch states, we obtain the block-diagonalized Hamiltonian consisting of block matrices of at most four dimensions. Partial of the eigenstates are analytically solved. For the six-site anisotropic ring, we reveal a subset of eigenstates that are simultaneous eigenstates of the Hamiltonian and the total angular momentum operator, even though the latter is not conserved. For both the six- and eight-site isotropic rings, we achieve momentum-space manifestations of several important states, including the famous Majumdar-Ghosh (MG) ground states and the Hamada-Kane-Nakagawa-Natsume (HKNN) ground state. The equivalence of these states with their real-space counterparts is explicitly shown for $N=6$. The structure of the HKNN ground state for small rings suggests that for any even number $N$ this state might behave like a ``bound state" with $N/2$ successive down spins binding together.

</details>


### [3] [Grassmann time-evolving matrix product operators for fermionic impurities coupled to a superconducting bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23301)
*Chu Guo,Wei Wu,Xiansong Xu,Ping-Xing Chen,Changming Yue,Tian Jiang,Ruofan Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文扩展GTEMPO方法至Nambu形式体系，通过Bogoliubov变换处理超导库，实现了对费米子杂质问题在超导库环境下的高效求解，并通过多种基准测试验证了精度与灵活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将GTEMPO方法从正常库扩展至超导库（Nambu形式体系），以解决更广泛的费米子杂质问题，特别是超导库环境下的非平衡动力学和DMFT求解。

Method: 采用Bogoliubov变换将超导库映射为类似正常库的形式，得到Feynman-Vernon影响泛函的解析表达式，从而将GTEMPO的核心算法直接适配到Nambu形式体系。

Result: 在精确可解案例上与精确对角化比对，在不可积案例上与连续时间量子蒙特卡洛方法（CTQMC）比对，均验证了精度；同时展示了虚时和实时计算的灵活性。

Conclusion: 该方法有望成为DMFT及其非平衡推广在处理Nambu形式体系费米子杂质问题时的有效杂质求解器。

Abstract: The Grassmann time-evolving matrix product operator (GTEMPO) method, which represents the Feynman-Vernon influence functional as a temporal matrix product state, has been shown to be a flexible and potentially scalable solution for fermionic quantum impurity problems. In this work, we extend GTEMPO to solve fermionic impurity problems in the Nambu formalism, in which the impurity is coupled to a superconducting bath. A key insight is that by employing the Bogoliubov transformation for the superconducting bath, one could obtain the analytic expression of the Feynman-Vernon influence functional in a similar form to the case of a normal bath, after which the core algorithms of GTEMPO can be straightforwardly adapted. We demonstrate the accuracy of our method by benchmarking it against exact diagonalization in several exactly solvable cases, and against the continuous-time quantum Monte Carlo method using converged dynamical mean field theory (DMFT) iterations on the imaginary contour in the non-integrable case. In all cases, we perform both imaginary- and real-time calculations to illustrate the flexibility of our method. These results illustrate that our method could be potentially useful as an impurity solver in DMFT as well as its non-equilibrium extension for fermionic impurity problems in the Nambu formalism.

</details>


### [4] [Coherent spin waves in a maximal entropy phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23597)
*Arnau Romaguera,Eugenio Paris,Elizabeth Skoropata,Stefano Agrestini,Mirian Garcia-Fernandez,Marisa Medarde,Noah Schnitzer,Lopa Bhatt,Berit H. Goodge,Yun Yen,Matthias Krack,Michael Schüler,Romain Sibille,Tom Fennell,Daniel G. Mazzone,Jakob Lass,Ellen Fogh,Anirudha Ghosh,Marco Caputo,Carlos William Galdino,Zhijia Zhang,Thorsten Schmitt,Milan Radovic,Luc Patthey,Hiroki Ueda,Monica Ciomaga Hatnean,Elia Razzoli*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文发现反铁磁材料YBaCuFeO5中，熵驱动的混合相使无序反而增强了自旋波的相干性，挑战了传统认为无序会破坏集体激发的认知。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试无序是否必然破坏磁性系统中相干集体激发的传统认知，探索高熵材料中熵稳定混合相能否维持甚至增强自旋波的相干性。

Method: 选取具有两种不同磁矩过渡金属原子的反铁磁YBaCuFeO5，结合共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）和线性自旋波理论进行实验与理论分析。

Result: 在熵驱动的混合相中，自旋波保持色散特性，具有清晰的声学和光学分支，且两者之间存在较大的光学能隙，与有序基态预期显著不同。

Conclusion: 在熵稳定磁体中，无序可以促进之前认为仅存在于低熵系统中的相干集体模式，颠覆了“无序必然削弱相干性”的传统观点。

Abstract: In solids, disorder is conventionally regarded as detrimental to coherence. It typically localizes and dampens collective excitations, as exemplified by Anderson localization or the broadening of magnetic modes in systems lacking long-range order. While high-entropy materials are specifically designed to harness disorder and stabilize homogeneous mixed-phase structures that can display unique properties, this same disorder is nonetheless expected to preclude the formation of coherent magnetic excitations. To test the limits of this picture, we selected the antiferromagnetic system YBaCuFeO5, as it features two distinct transition metal atoms with significantly different magnetic moments, rendering its spin dynamics exceptionally sensitive to local atomic ordering. Combining resonant inelastic x-ray scattering and linear spin wave theory, we reveal a surprising paradox: YBaCuFeO5 exhibits an unexpected, entropy-driven mixed phase, in which disorder, rather than reducing the lifetime of the collective excitations, favors coherence. In this mixed phase, the spin waves remain dispersive, markedly distinct from those expected for an ordered ground state, and exhibit well-defined acoustic and optical branches separated by a large optical gap. These results demonstrate that in entropy-stabilized magnets, disorder can favor coherent collective modes previously thought to be exclusive to low-entropy systems.

</details>


### [5] [Testing the robustness of topological quantities evaluated from the modular Hamiltonian for a given wavefunction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24058)
*Sandeep Sharma,Ajit C. Balram*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用基于模哈密顿量的方法，从分数量子霍尔态的晶格模型中提取拓扑序的拓扑量子数（如霍尔电导、拓扑纠缠熵、手征中心荷），并在玻色型Laughlin态和Moore-Read态上验证了该方法，发现结果收敛到预期值，但收敛速度与关联长度成反比，且需要大系统尺寸才能可靠提取拓扑内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑序是量子多体系统中重要的概念，但如何从波函数中可靠提取拓扑量子数是一个关键问题。本文旨在验证基于模哈密顿量的方法在晶格模型（分数量子霍尔态）上的有效性，并探讨其收敛性条件和系统尺寸要求。

Method: 采用模哈密顿量方法，在晶格模型中分别对玻色型Laughlin态和Moore-Read态进行数值计算，提取霍尔电导、拓扑纠缠熵和手征中心荷等拓扑量子数，并通过改变系统尺寸和关联长度来分析收敛行为。

Result: 该方法成功提取了预期的拓扑量子数，且结果收敛。但收敛速度与状态的关联长度有关：关联长度越长，收敛越慢。此外，可靠提取需要足够大的系统尺寸。

Conclusion: 基于模哈密顿量的方法可以有效地从分数量子霍尔态的晶格模型中提取拓扑序的拓扑内容，但实际应用中需要注意系统尺寸和关联长度对收敛性的影响，以保证结果的可靠性。

Abstract: Topologically ordered states are characterized by topological quantities like the Hall conductance, topological entanglement entropy, and chiral central charge. Techniques based on the modular Hamiltonian have recently been developed to extract these quantities from a wavefunction. Here, we consider a lattice model of fractional quantum Hall states, a prototypical example of topologically ordered systems, and extract their topological content using the modular Hamiltonian-based methods. We consider the bosonic Laughlin and Moore-Read states and show that the extracted topological quantum numbers converge to their expected results. As expected, the convergence is slower when the correlation length of the state is longer. Generally, our results show that a reliable extraction of topological content through modular methods requires the usage of large systems

</details>


### [6] [Dichroic Raman probes for chiral edge modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24208)
*Avedis Neehus,Johannes Knolle*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文发现，在Kitaev量子自旋液体中，闭合边界固有的长程关联无序可以导致拉曼圆二色性信号，该信号避免了线性与角动量选择规则的抑制，并展现出依赖于实验可调长度和能量尺度的特征，从而能够探测到原本拉曼非活性的手性边缘模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，识别和操控电中性分数化准粒子，特别是手性边缘模，是物理学中的一个长期追求的目标。由于手性边缘模因晶格动量守恒而拉曼非活性，拉曼探针被认为不适用于识别它们，因此需要找到新的探测方法。

Method: 以Kitaev量子自旋液体为例，通过理论计算，研究了闭合边界固有的长程关联无序如何导致拉曼圆二色性信号，分析了该信号对线性与角动量选择规则的规避机制，并计算了低频拉曼圆二色性响应。

Result: 发现了闭合边界的无序可以产生拉曼圆二色性信号，该信号不受动量选择规则抑制，且依赖于可调的长度和能量尺度；手性物质费米子与Z2边界电荷的相互作用通过各向异性塞曼场依赖留下了Kitaev量子自旋液体的独特指纹。

Conclusion: 拉曼圆二色性可用作探测Kitaev量子自旋液体中手性边缘模的有效工具，为识别电中性分数化准粒子提供了新途径。

Abstract: The identification and manipulation of charge-neutral fractionalized quasi-particles, in particular chiral edge modes (CEM), is a long-standing quest in physics. Remarkably, the microscopically mediated interaction between light and charge-neutral excitations in Mott-Hubbard insulators can take an identical form to the Raman coupling between light and particles with electric charge. However, since CEMs are Raman-inactive due to conservation of lattice momentum, Raman probes have been deemed unsuitable for their identification. Here, using the Kitaev quantum spin liquid (KSL) as an illustrative example, we demonstrate that the long-range correlated disorder inherent to a closed edge can lead to a Raman circular dichroism (RCD) signal that avoids suppression by linear and angular momentum selection rules, and exhibits a dependence on experimentally tunable length and energy scales that are characteristic of CEM. Having calculated the low-frequency RCD response of generic KSL, we argue that the interaction of the chiral matter fermion with the $\Ztwo$ boundary charge leaves a unique fingerprint of the KSL via the anisotropic Zeeman field dependence.

</details>


### [7] [Umklapp corrections to Landau damping and conditions for non-trivial modifications to quantum critical transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24274)
*Vibhu Mishra*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文计算了d=2维度下Ising向列金属中临界费米面接近布里渊区边界时的粒子-空穴气泡，发现除了标准的对映贡献外，还存在来自近边界电子的Umklapp贡献，其标度行为取决于温度，并讨论了该贡献对线性电阻率激活温度的潜在影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Ising向列金属中临界费米面接近布里渊区边界时的粒子-空穴气泡行为，特别是Umklapp过程对量子临界输运性质的影响，以理解其对电阻率温度依赖性的修正。

Method: 在d=2和d=3维度下，分别计算粒子-空穴泡的两种贡献：标准对映部分(Π_ATP)和Umklapp部分(Π_U)。对d=2情形，分析不同温度下Umklapp贡献的标度指数α（2/3或1/2），并讨论其对线性电阻率激活温度T_U的影响。

Result: d=2时：标准对映部分Π_ATP ∝ Ω/q；Umklapp部分在最小Umklapp动量q≈Δ_q处，Π_U ∝ Ω^α，其中高温时α=1/2，低温时α=2/3。高温下（α=1/2），T_U可能从z=3临界性预期的T_U∝Δ_q^3降低为T_U∝Δ_q^4。d=3时：Π_U∼Ω与温度无关，因此T_U不变。

Conclusion: Umklapp贡献仅在d=2且高温（α=1/2）的特殊条件下可能降低线性电阻率的激活温度，但该场景非常特定；d=3情况下Umklapp过程对T_U无影响。

Abstract: We compute the particle--hole bubble for an Ising-nematic metal when the critical Fermi surface approaches the Brillouin zone boundary for $d=2$ dimensions. We find two qualitatively distinct contributions: i)~the standard antipodal piece, which gives $Π_{\rm{ATP}}(\mathbf{q}, iΩ)\proptoΩ/q$ and ii)~an additional umklapp piece from electrons near the zone boundary, which gives $Π_{\rm{U}}(\mathbf{q}, iΩ)\propto Ω^α$ at the minimum umklapp momentum $q\approx Δ_q$ with $α= 2/3 $ or $1/2$ depending on the temperature $T$. At high $T$ when $α= 1/2$, the minimum $T$ for the activation of linear/quasi-linear in $T$ resistivity, which is expected to be $T_U \propto Δ_q^3$ from $z=3$ criticality, could potentially get reduced to $T_U \propto Δ_q^4$ due to the $\sqrtΩ$ term and discuss why we find only one hyper-specific scenario where this possibility might be realized. For $d=3$ the umklapp contribution gives $Π_{\rm{U}}\sim Ω$ irrespective of $T$ therefore $T_U$ is not modified in this case.

</details>


### [8] [Field-induced jammed polyhex spin liquid in the honeycomb Ising antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24687)
*Nicholas Franklin,Jacob Richards,Harry Lane*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了蜂窝状伊辛反铁磁体在外磁场中的基态性质，发现有限磁场下存在大量基态简并，映射为多六边形平铺问题，形成阻塞自旋液体态，并通过蒙特卡洛模拟和量子涨落分析展示了其性质及实验可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究蜂窝状伊辛反铁磁体在外加磁场中的基态性质，特别是基态简并度及其物理表现。

Method: 理论分析将基态简并映射为多六边形平铺问题；通过蒙特卡洛模拟探索自旋扩散等性质；引入量子涨落分析横向耦合对简并度的影响。

Result: 发现有限磁场下存在大量基态简并，形成阻塞自旋液体态（无局域零模）；蒙特卡洛模拟显示自旋扩散可由磁场强度调控；量子涨落下横向耦合部分解除简并，选择出12六边形的非周期平铺子空间。

Conclusion: 阻塞多六边形自旋液体相存在于实验可实现的参数区域，可能在FePX₃化合物中被观测到。

Abstract: We analyze the ground state properties of the honeycomb Ising antiferromagnet in an external magnetic field. We demonstrate the existence of extensive ground state degeneracy at finite field that maps to a polyhex tiling problem. This state is shown to be a jammed spin liquid, with no local zero modes connecting ground states. Through Monte Carlo simulations, we explore the properties of these states and show that the spin diffusion can be controlled by the magnetic field strength. By considering quantum fluctuations, we demonstrate that transverse coupling partially lifts the ground state degeneracy, selecting an extensive subspace of non-periodic tilings of 12-hexes. We suggest that the jammed polyhex spin liquid phase exists in an experimentally realizable region of parameter space and may be present in the FePX$_3$ compounds.

</details>


### [9] [Control of the Néel vector in the quantum antiferromagnetic honeycomb lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24695)
*Asliddin Khudoyberdiev,Dag-Björn Hering,Vanessa Sulaiman,Götz S. Uhrig*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明了时间相关Schwinger玻色子平均场理论能够有效描述低对称性量子反铁磁体（如蜂窝晶格）中的奈尔矢量翻转过程，揭示了晶格配位数与阈值翻转场之间的对应关系，为超快自旋电子学或磁振子学器件的发展奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展并验证时间相关Schwinger玻色子平均场理论在低对称性量子反铁磁体中的适用性，以推动反铁磁翻转的基础研究。

Method: 采用时间相关Schwinger玻色子平均场理论，通过分析蜂窝晶格的平衡性质（与连续相似性变换方法对比）及其在翻转过程中的动力学行为，系统研究不同晶格配位数下的阈值翻转场。

Result: 发现了晶格结构（蜂窝晶格与正方晶格、简单立方晶格）与阈值翻转场之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为未来反铁磁翻转的理论与计算研究奠定了基础，对超快自旋电子学/磁振子学器件开发具有重要意义。

Abstract: The switching of antiferromagnetic order and its efficient control promise to enable ultrafast manipulation of data and large storage capacity. Recently, the time-dependent Schwinger boson mean-field theory has been successfully developed to study the Néel vector switching in hypercubic antiferromagnetic lattices. In the present article, we aim at demonstrating that the approach is a well-justified framework to capture the essentials of the switching process, even in low-symmetry quantum antiferromagnets. To this end, we show the possibility of the sublattice magnetization reorientation in the quantum antiferromagnetic honeycomb lattice. First, equilibrium properties of the honeycomb lattice are analyzed using the Schwinger boson mean-field theory and compared to the continuous similarity transformation method to justify the applicability of the approach. Then, the Schwinger boson mean-field theory is employed for switching process. We provide a comprehensive answer to the question what the threshold switching fields are when the coordination number of the lattice is varied. Indeed, the results of the study reveal a correspondence between lattice structures and the threshold fields by comparing them for the square and the simple cubic lattices and the honeycomb lattice. The findings of the present article extend the foundation for future theoretical and computational advancements in the field of antiferromagnetic switching. These advancements are of particular relevance for the development of ultrafast spintronic or magnonic devices.

</details>


### [10] [Non-Abelian Particle-Loop, Fracton, and Planon Condensation in Cage-Net Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24755)
*Yifei Wang,Yu Zhao,Yingcheng Li,Hao Song,Yidun Wan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于HGW弦网模型解耦层构建扩展笼网分数量子（fracton）模型的框架，实现了非阿贝尔p-loop、fracton和planon的凝聚。通过构建凝聚投影算子，展示了在扩展Ising笼网模型中凝聚非阿贝尔(σσ̄,1)-环可驱动相变至X-cube模型，并揭示了fracton和planon凝聚导致的不同退耦行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有笼网模型基于Levin-Wen弦网模型，无法完整描述准粒子的内部空间（缺少tail自由度）。本文旨在构建一个更一般的框架，通过HGW弦网模型（具有tail自由度）来扩展笼网模型，从而实现非阿贝尔任意子的p-loop凝聚、fracton凝聚和planon凝聚，并建立不同分数量子序之间的哈密顿量相变机制。

Method: 利用解耦的HGW弦网模型层构建扩展笼网分数量子模型，通过投影父代2D HGW层的准粒子谱导出笼网模型的准粒子谱；构建(σσ̄,1)-环的凝聚投影算子；分析不同凝聚类型对系统序的影响。

Result: (1) 凝聚非阿贝尔(σ σ̄,1)-环将扩展Ising笼网模型映射到截断立方格点上的X-cube模型，揭示了非阿贝尔planon分裂为不同子维度激发；(2) fracton凝聚使3D分数量子序退耦回孤立的2D拓扑序层；(3) planon凝聚使系统完全塌缩为平凡相。

Conclusion: 建立了不同分数量子序之间的哈密顿量相变的具体机制，提供了一种可推广的分析子维度激发演化的方法，对理解高维拓扑序与分数量子序的相互关系具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present a framework for non-Abelian p-loop, fracton, and planon condensation in 3+1 dimensions by constructing extended cage-net fracton models using decoupled layers of the Hu-Geer-Wu (HGW) string-net model. These cage-net models extend the conventional cage-net models based on the Levin-Wen (LW) string-net model in the sense that they inherit the tail degrees of freedom of the HGW models, which are essential for completely describing the internal spaces of quasiparticles. This approach allows us to explicitly derive the quasiparticle spectra of the cage-net models by projecting those of the parent 2D HGW layers. Utilizing this framework, we can condense the p-loops formed by non-Abelian anyons within a fracton phase. Specifically, we construct the condensation projector for $(σ\barσ, 1)$-loops within the extended Ising Cage-Net (ICN) model. We demonstrate that condensing these non-Abelian loops drives a phase transition that maps the ICN model to the X-cube (XC) model defined on a truncated cubic lattice, a process that explicitly reveals the splitting of non-Abelian planons into distinct sub-dimensional excitations. Furthermore, our framework extends to the condensation of fractons and planons: we demonstrate that in the ICN model fracton condensation drives the decoupling of the 3D fracton order back into isolated 2D topological order layers, while planon condensation collapses the system entirely into a trivial phase. Our results establish a concrete Hamiltonian mechanism for phase transitions between distinct fracton orders and provide a generalizable method for analyzing the evolution of sub-dimensional excitations.

</details>

### [11] [Delocalization transition for light in two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22919)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战二维体系中任意弱无序必然导致本征模空间局域化的传统理论共识，探究近场偶极-偶极相互作用能否驱动局域化-退局域化转变。

Method: 理论分析二维平行板波导中随机分布两能级原子的光散射系统，利用有限尺寸标度分析估计临界指数。

Abstract: Common belief, confirmed by existing experiments, is that arbitrarily weak disorder should lead to spatial localization of eigenmodes of scalar wave equations when wave propagation is two-dimensional (2D). We predict that contrary to this belief, a localization-delocalization transition can take place for light scattered by two-level atoms placed at random positions in the middle plane of a parallel-plate 2D waveguide fed by its fundamental transverse-magnetic (TM) mode (electric field polarized perpendicular to the waveguide and atomic planes). This transition, driven by near-field dipole-dipole interactions between atoms, occurs upon increasing the areal number density of atoms beyond some critical value. A finite-size scaling analysis of the transition yields an estimate of its critical exponent $ν$ = 1.4 $\pm$ 0.2.

### [13] [Physics-Informed Deep Image Prior Reconstruction of In-Plane Magnetization from Scanning NV Magnetometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23431)
*Zander Scholl,Justin Woods,Charudatta Phatak,Hanu Arava*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出利用物理信息驱动的深度图像先验（DIP）框架，结合卷积自编码器，从扫描NV磁力测量数据中重建纳米尺度磁性薄膜的复杂面内磁化分布，无需预训练数据集且计算量较低。研究发现用户定义掩模的取向对重建收敛性有显著影响，最佳取向可提升信噪比达3 dB。该方法在光刻坡莫合金纳米结构中进行了实验验证，并辅以磁力显微镜测量支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度磁性薄膜的磁化重建对下一代存储、传感器和自旋电子技术至关重要，但杂散场逆问题存在病态性（无穷多解），传统方法难以实现准确重建。

Method: 采用物理信息驱动的深度图像先验（DIP）框架，使用简单卷积自编码器结构；通过用户定义掩模约束解空间，并优化掩模取向；结合实验引导的空间约束分析Landau和偶极畴结构。

Result: DIP框架能够实现复杂面内磁化模式的定性和定量重建；掩模取向显著影响收敛性，最优取向可将重建信噪比提升最多3 dB；该方法无需预训练数据集，计算成本低于监督学习方法。

Conclusion: 物理信息驱动的DIP框架为纳米尺度磁化重建提供了一种无需预训练数据的有效方案，掩模取向优化可作为诊断工具，该方法在实验数据上得到验证。

Abstract: Reconstructing magnetization in nanoscale magnetic thin films is essential for developing next-generation memory, sensors, and various spintronic technologies. However, this remains challenging due to the ill-posed nature of the stray field inverse problem, i.e., there are infinitely many magnetization solutions to a given stray field distribution. Here, we demonstrate that a physics-informed deep image prior (DIP) framework, using a simple convolutional autoencoder conditionally achieves a reasonable qualitative and quantitative reconstruction of complex in-plane magnetization patterns from scanning NV magnetometry. We find that the orientation of user-defined masks implemented to restrict the reconstruction solution space dramatically affects convergence. The optimal alignment of the mask improves the reconstruction signal-to-noise ratio by up to $\SI{3}{\decibel}$, thereby also serving as a diagnostic tool. The DIP approach requires no pre-trained datasets and is considered computationally less intensive as compared to supervised learning approaches. We analyze both Landau and dipole domain structures in lithographically patterned Permalloy nanostructures by incorporating experimentally-guided spatial constraints. Complementary magnetic force microscopy measurements were carried out to support the Scanning NV measurements.

### [14] [Bayesian phase transition for the critical Ising model: Enlarged replica symmetry in the epsilon expansion and in 2D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23346)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究临界Ising模型中测量键能的精度如何导致不同的测量"相"，特别是进入强测量相的相变机制及其普适性质。

Method: 采用复制场论（围绕六维的ε展开）和二维数值模拟，分析关联函数的多标度行为，并研究长程相互作用/测量情况下的ε展开。

Abstract: A process that images or measures bond energies in the critical Ising model can be in distinct measurement ``phases'', depending on the precision of measurement. We study the transition into the strong-measurement phase using replica field theory (an epsilon expansion around six dimensions) and numerical simulations in two dimensions. The results reveal multiscaling of correlation functions at the critical point, and a striking enlarged symmetry of the replica description. This is an analog of the Nishimori phenomenon in the Ising spin glass, in a distinct replica limit. The enlarged symmetry is present microscopically for certain measurement protocols, but more generally can emerge in the infrared, and it fixes the exact value of the exponent for the Edwards-Anderson correlator both in 2D and near the upper critical dimension. We also examine the epsilon expansion for models with power-law interactions and/or long-range measurement.

### [15] [Beyond average: heterogeneous first-passage dynamics in many-particle systems with resetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24406)
*Juhee Lee,Seong-Gyu Yang,Ludvig Lizana*

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了随机重置对多粒子相互作用系统中首次通过过程的影响，发现集体重置会导致到达时间分布呈现重尾特征和多个数量级的平台期，平均到达时间随重置率增加而发散，系统缺乏单一特征时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机重置在单粒子动力学中已有充分理解，但其对多粒子集体行为的影响尚不清楚。作者受到人工选择和规避问题的启发，研究了一种特殊协议：所有存活粒子被重置到最极端粒子的位置。

Method: 采用随机模拟方法，研究在约束势阱中扩散并具有吸收边界的粒子系统。考虑两种到达定义：首个粒子到达边界和半数粒子到达边界。实施将所有存活粒子重置到最极端粒子位置的协议。

Result: 重置产生具有重尾和延伸平台期（跨越多个数量级）的宽到达时间分布。平均到达时间随重置率增加而增长，并在超过阈值后发散。轨迹级分析显示强异质性，存在极短和极长的吸收时间。

Conclusion: 集体重置缺乏单一特征时间尺度，到达的定义对于理解和控制此类系统至关重要。

Abstract: We study how stochastic resetting affects first-passage processes in systems of many interacting particles. While resetting is well understood for single-particle dynamics, its consequences for collective behavior remain less clear. We consider a protocol in which all surviving particles are reset to the position of the most extreme one, motivated by problems in artificial selection and avoidance. Using stochastic simulations of particles diffusing in a confining potential with an absorbing boundary, we examine two notions of arrival: when the first particle reaches the boundary and the point at which half of the particles do. We find that resetting produces broad distributions of arrival times with heavy tails and extended plateaus that span several orders of magnitude. As the resetting rate increases, the mean arrival time grows and diverges beyond a threshold. Trajectory-level analysis also reveals strong heterogeneity, with very short and very long absorption times. These results show that collective resetting lacks a single characteristic time scale and that the definition of arrival is crucial for understanding and controlling such systems.

Abstract: We present a technique to investigate the stationary states of a system of a collisionless system confined by an external potential and coupled to boundary reservoirs through prescribed reinjection rules. We consider a family of boundary conditions parametrized by an integer $n$, corresponding to different velocity distributions imposed at the boundaries, generalizing the standard flux-weighted Maxwellian scheme. By combining Liouville's theorem with the boundary injection rule, we derive an explicit analytical expression for the stationary distribution function. This framework provides a direct link between microscopic boundary dynamics and macroscopic stationary profiles. We show that thermal equilibrium is recovered only for the standard flux-weighted injection method, while for all other cases the system relaxes to manifestly non-thermal stationary states. The resulting density and temperature profiles exhibit non-trivial spatial structures, including non-monotonic behaviour and temperature gradients induced by the boundary conditions alone. Analytical predictions for stationary moments are obtained in closed form for representative cases and are nicely reproduced by particle-based numerical simulations.

Abstract: Conformal symmetry is expected to be realized in many equilibrium statistical mechanical systems at criticality. ### [19] [On the geometric algebras of the Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24688)
*N. Johnson,D. Marenduzzo,A. Morozov,E. Orlandini,G. M. Vasil*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从克利福德和共形几何代数的视角重新审视了伊辛模型的转移矩阵解法，将转移矩阵、本征矢量和准粒子激发统一解释为共形克利福德代数的元素，揭示了伊辛模型与自由马约拉纳费米子理论之间的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为伊辛模型的经典转移矩阵解法提供一个统一的几何代数框架，以更紧凑、物理可解释的方式阐明其中的尺度变换、费米子模式和对偶性等核心概念，作为传统费米子、格拉斯曼或场论处理方式的有益教学补充。

Method: 基于Kaufman的旋量形式，利用共形克利福德代数重新表述一维和二维伊辛模型的转移矩阵方法。将转移矩阵视为由共形双矢量生成的伸缩变换，将本征矢量视为克利福德生成元的零组合，在二维情形中将转移矩阵的本征值方程重新解释为准粒子激发的色散关系。

Result: 成功恢复所有已知的精确结果，并表明转移矩阵、本征矢量与准粒子激发均可统一在共形克利福德代数的框架下，揭示了伊辛模型与自由马约拉纳费米子理论之间的结构对应关系。

Conclusion: 这种几何代数的方法提供了一个紧凑、统一且物理可解释的代数框架，清晰地展示了伊辛模型中的尺度变换、费米子模式和对偶性，可作为传统处理方式的有效教学补充。

Abstract: We revisit the classical transfer matrix solution of the one- and two-dimensional Ising model from the perspective of Clifford and conformal geometric algebras. Building on Kaufman's spinor formulation, we show that all elements entering the solution, including the transfer matrix, its eigenvectors, and the quasiparticle excitations, admit a natural and unified interpretation as elements of an appropriate conformal Clifford algebra. In particular, the transfer matrix can be viewed as a dilation generated by a conformal bivector, while its eigenvectors correspond to null combinations of Clifford generators, closely paralleling the emergence of Majorana fermionic degrees of freedom. In the two-dimensional case, the standard eigenvalue equation for the row-to-row transfer matrix is reinterpreted as a dispersion relation for quasiparticle excitations, exposing the connection between the Ising model and a theory of free Majorana fermions. While all the explicit exact results recovered are well known, this geometric reformulation provides a unified algebraic framework which is compact and physically interpretable. Specifically, this clarifies the role of scale transformations, fermionic modes, and duality in the Ising model. We believe this approach offers a useful pedagogical complement to more conventional fermionic, Grassmann, or field theoretic treatments.

</details>


### [20] [Universal tracer statistics in single-file transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24741)
*Soumyabrata Saha,Jitendra Kethepalli,Benjamin Guiselin,Jacopo De Nardis,Tridib Sadhu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 在一维硬棒气体中，随机（扩散）和幺正（弹道）两种截然不同的微观动力学在大尺度长时间统计上表现出普适性——单时间多示踪子联合分布的非高斯涨落仅相差一个简单的动力学缩放因子。这种普适性在退火和淬火系综中都成立，而微观差异仅体现在多时间统计中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究两种本质上不同的微观动力学（随机扩散与幺正弹道）在大尺度长时间极限下是否具有统计行为的普适性，特别是非平衡多粒子系统中的涨落普适类问题。

Method: 通过精确微观求解和涨落流体力学（弹道情形退火系综）获得大偏差结果，结合稀有事件模拟进行验证。分析单时间双示踪子统计和单示踪子的双时间统计，并在淬火系综中研究流涨落。

Result: 发现两种动力学下单时间多示踪子联合分布的非高斯涨落完全一致（仅需简单动力学缩放）；差异仅出现在多时间统计中。退火和淬火系综均保持普适性，表明系统对初始状态具有持久记忆。

Conclusion: 揭示了一维硬棒气体中扩散与弹道动力学之间意想不到的普适类，为理解非平衡系统中微观动力学与宏观涨落统计之间的关系提供了新视角。

Abstract: We uncover an emergent universality in the large-scale, long-time statistics of a one-dimensional hard-rod gas evolving under two fundamentally different classes of microscopic dynamics: stochastic (diffusive) and unitary (ballistic). Remarkably, despite the difference of the two systems, the one-time joint distribution of the positions of multiple tracers exhibits identical non-Gaussian fluctuations, up to a simple dynamical scaling. This universality holds in both annealed and quenched ensembles, demonstrating a persistent memory of the initial state. Differences between the dynamics manifest at large scales only in multi-time statistics. Our conclusions are based on explicit large-deviation results for the one-time statistics of tracer pairs and the two-time statistics of a single tracer. Similar physics extends to current fluctuations, demonstrated explicitly in the quenched ensemble. We obtain these results from exact microscopic solutions for both dynamics and, independently, from fluctuating hydrodynamics in the ballistic case in the annealed ensemble. Our rare-event simulations further corroborate these findings and provide a novel demonstration of sampling atypical fluctuations in both types of hard-rod gas.

### [21] [Deterministic Multi-User Identification over Bosonic Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22804)
*Gökhan Elmas,Janis Nötzel*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于相干态签名的玻色子信道确定性多用户识别问题。每个用户被分配一个满足平均能量约束的相干乘积态，通过用户特定的二元量子测试进行识别。与基于共享码本的经典多用户识别模型不同，该方案将每个接收器与高维相空间中的几何签名关联。利用度量熵界，证明了识别容量呈现近k log k的标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子通信中多用户识别的新范式，突破传统基于码本共享的经典识别模型限制，利用量子态几何特性实现更高效的用户识别。

Method: 采用相干态签名方案，每个用户分配满足平均能量约束的相干乘积态；通过用户特定的二元量子测试进行识别；利用度量熵界分析识别容量标度行为。

Result: 证明了识别容量呈现近k log k的标度行为，其中k为用户数量。

Conclusion: 该工作将多用户识别问题从传统的码本共享范式扩展到量子几何签名范式，为量子多用户通信提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We study deterministic multi-user identification over bosonic channels using coherent-state signatures. Each user is assigned a coherent product state under an average energy constraint, and identification is performed by a user-specific binary quantum test. In contrast to classical multi-user identification models based on shared codebooks, this formulation associates each receiver with a geometric signature in high-dimensional phase space. Using metric entropy bounds, we show that the identification capacity exhibits a near-k log k scaling behavior.

### [22] [Bell Inequalities from Polyhedral Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22859)
*Christian Staufenbiel*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出邻接采样方法（Adjacency Sampling），在牺牲完备性的前提下大幅加速贝尔不等式的枚举，在已知场景中复现所有不等式类，在未完全求解场景中将结果提升数十倍至数百万类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝尔不等式在量子关联认证和设备无关量子密钥分发中至关重要，但完整枚举所有贝尔不等式在计算上极其困难（需解决关联贝尔多面体的面枚举问题），因此需要高效的近似枚举方法。

Method: 基于邻接分解方法（Adjacency Decomposition），但牺牲完备性以换取速度，即邻接采样方法。

Result: 在已知场景中复现所有不等式类；在 $\mathcal{L}_{3,3,3,3}$ 中获得超过 $1.29 \times 10^8$ 类（提升25倍以上）；在 $\mathcal{L}_{4,5,2,2}$ 中接近翻三倍至49,358类；在 $\mathcal{L}_{4,6,2,2}$ 中报告超过430万类。

Conclusion: 邻接采样方法能够高效发现大量新的贝尔不等式类，显著扩展了可处理场景的规模，为量子关联研究提供了更丰富的工具。

Abstract: Bell inequalities play a central role in certifying quantum correlations and underpin protocols such as device-independent quantum key distribution. However, enumerating all Bell inequalities for a given scenario remains intractable beyond the simplest cases, as it requires solving a computationally hard facet enumeration problem on the associated Bell polytope. We propose the Adjacency Sampling method, which builds on the Adjacency Decomposition method but sacrifices completeness for speed. On previously solved Bell polytopes, the method reproduces every known class of inequalities. For scenarios where no complete enumeration exists, it greatly exceeds existing partial results: in $\mathcal{L}_{3,3,3,3}$ we obtain over $1.29 \times 10^8$ classes, more than 25 times the previous count; in $\mathcal{L}_{4,5,2,2}$ we nearly triple the known list to 49\,358 classes; and for $\mathcal{L}_{4,6,2,2}$ we report over 4.3 million classes.

</details>

Result: IA-QCNN以极低的可训练参数数量实现高预测精度，有效缓解过拟合；T1Gd模态判别力优于mpMRI；模型在混合噪声环境中表现出卓越鲁棒性，噪声可作为正则化机制提升预测性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的IA-QCNN架构为处理异质性放射基因组学数据提供了经典方法之外的一种鲁棒且计算高效的替代方案，建立了GBM放射基因组学与量子深度学习之间的方法论桥梁。

Although various AI frameworks have been developed for non-invasive MGMT prediction, spatial heterogeneity of methylation status and the high-dimensional and correlated nature of MRI data frequently constrain discriminative feature learning and generalizability of classical models. To circumvent these limitations, a specialized IA-QCNN architecture is proposed, based on the principles of quantum mechanics, including superposition and entanglement, and enabling more efficient representation learning in high-dimensional Hilbert space. The framework establishes a methodological bridge between GBM radiogenomics and quantum deep learning by integrating energy-based slice selection, importance-aware weighting, ring-topology quantum convolution, and folding-based pooling layers. When the model predicts MGMT promoter methylation status using both mpMRI and T1Gd images, experimental results demonstrate that the IA-QCNN achieves high accuracy despite its low number of trainable parameters while effectively minimizing the overfitting problem observed in classical models. Quantitative analyses reveal that the T1Gd modality possesses higher discriminative power than mpMRI, establishing a clinically significant sequence preference. Furthermore, the model exhibits exceptional robustness in hybrid noise environments, effectively utilizing noise as a regularization mechanism to enhance predictive performance. Consequently, the specialized IA-QCNN architecture provides a robust and computationally efficient alternative to classical approaches in the analysis of heterogeneous radiogenomic data.

### [24] [Charging Dynamics in a Distance-Modulated Planar Quantum-Battery Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22878)
*Yi-Fan Yang,Shun-Cai Zhao*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由耦合谐振子构成的平面多体量子电池架构，通过引入距离依赖函数调控电池间耦合与隧穿，利用Redfield主方程研究强耦合下的充放电动力学。结果表明：最佳距离窗口内减小间距可抑制充电波动并加速稳态，但过短距离会放大环境耗散；适度耦合能平衡最大储能与稳定性；系统-浴耦合和截止频率主导充电时间尺度，且该架构在宽温区内对热涨落保持鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子电池理论模型很少明确考虑几何依赖的相互作用，而空间排列对量子电池的物理实现至关重要，因此有必要研究几何结构对充电性能的影响。

Method: 提出平面多体量子电池架构（耦合谐振子），引入距离依赖函数调制电池间耦合与隧穿，采用Redfield主方程方法研究强耦合下的开放系统充电动力学，以ergotropy为主要性能指标。

Result: 1）减小最佳窗口内的电池间距可抑制充电波动并加速达到稳态；2）过短间距会放大环境耗散，降低性能；3）过强耦合导致充电后不稳定性，适度耦合可实现最大储能与稳定性的平衡；4）系统-浴耦合和截止频率主导充电时间尺度；5）平面架构在宽温区内对热涨落保持鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 几何控制的相互作用在多体量子电池中起关键作用，该结果为二维量子储能器件的设计与优化提供了理论基础。

Abstract: While the spatial arrangement of individual units is essential for the physical implementation of quantum batteries, geometry-dependent interactions are rarely explicitly incorporated into existing theoretical models. To address this, we propose a planar many-body quantum-battery architecture consisting of coupled resonators. By introducing a distance-dependent function to modulate both the inter-battery coupling and tunneling, we investigate the open-system charging dynamics in the strong-coupling regime using a Redfield master-equation approach. Using ergotropy as the primary figure of merit, we demonstrate that the charging performance is highly sensitive to the inter-battery distance, nearest-neighbor coupling strength, and environmental conditions. Specifically, decreasing the inter-battery distance within an optimal window suppresses charging fluctuations and accelerates the system's approach to a steady charged state. However, an excessively short distance amplifies environmental dissipation, thereby degrading the overall performance. Furthermore, while overly strong inter-battery coupling induces post-charging instability, moderate coupling achieves a favorable balance between maximum stored energy and stability. We also establish that the system-bath coupling and bath cutoff frequency predominantly govern the charging timescale, and that the planar architecture maintains its robustness against thermal fluctuations over a broad temperature range. These results highlight the critical role of geometry-controlled interactions in many-body quantum batteries, providing a theoretical foundation for the design and optimization of two-dimensional quantum energy-storage devices.

</details>


### [25] [Quantum Dynamics and Collapse-and-Revival Phenomena in the Dunkl Anharmonic Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22945)
*D. Ojeda-Guillén,R. D. Mota,M. Salazar-Ramírez*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用SU(1,1)群的代数方法研究了Dunkl非谐振子（Kerr介质）哈密顿量，通过Dunkl产生湮灭算符得到精确能谱，并分析了Dunkl参数对量子动力学中崩塌与复兴现象、分数复兴、完美态重构以及压缩态的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在从SU(1,1)群的代数角度研究Dunkl非谐振子（Kerr介质）哈密顿量，以获得其精确能谱并揭示Dunkl变形对量子动力学行为（如崩塌与复兴、态重构、压缩态）的调制作用。

Method: 将哈密顿量用Dunkl产生湮灭算符表示，该算符闭合su(1,1)李代数；利用该代数结构精确求解能谱；以偶奇Dunkl相干态的叠加为初始态，计算场正交分量和生存概率，分析量子动力学；通过正交分量的方差分析压缩特性。

Result: 获得了宇称依赖的精确能谱；Dunkl参数μ调制分数复兴现象，并在特定变形值下在半周期处实现完美态重构；Dunkl变形在t≈π附近产生干涉诱导的压缩态；μ→0时恢复标准Kerr介质动力学。

Conclusion: Dunkl变形为调控Kerr介质的量子动力学行为（特别是态重构和压缩）提供了新的自由度，SU(1,1)代数方法是处理这类问题的有效工具。

Abstract: We study the Dunkl anharmonic oscillator (Kerr medium) Hamiltonian from an algebraic approach of the $SU(1,1)$ group. In order to obtain the exact energy spectrum of this problem, we write its Hamiltonian in terms of the Dunkl creation and annihilation operators, which close the $su(1,1)$ Lie algebra. This allows us to exactly solve this Hamiltonian and obtain its parity-dependent energy spectrum. Then, we investigate the quantum dynamics of the system, particularly the collapse and revival phenomena, by using an initial state given by a superposition of even and odd Dunkl coherent states. We compute the field quadrature and the survival probability, showing that the Dunkl parameter $μ$ modulates the fractional revivals and produces perfect state reconstructions at half-periods for specific deformation values. We analyze the quadrature variance to show that the Dunkl deformation generates interference-induced squeezed states around $t \approx π$. The standard Kerr medium dynamics are exactly recovered in the limit $μ\rightarrow 0$.

### [26] [No cloning with unitary scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22960)
*Dafa Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一般化的量子不可克隆原理，指出无法通过酉演化任意未知量子纯态的U-拷贝（即U|ψ⟩），将原始不可克隆原理从恒等拷贝扩展到了任意酉变换下的拷贝。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的比特串信息可以被复制，但1982年Wootters和Zurek提出的量子不可克隆原理表明，无法通过酉演化对任意未知量子纯态进行完全相同的复制。本文旨在将该原理推广到更一般的情形，即考虑任意酉变换下的拷贝（U-拷贝）是否同样不可实现。

Method: 论文从理论上定义了U-拷贝的概念：对于任意酉算子U，称U|ψ⟩为|ψ⟩的U-拷贝。在此基础上，论证了通过酉演化无法实现对任意未知量子纯态进行U-拷贝，从而建立了广义的不可克隆原理。

Result: 得出了广义不可克隆原理：无法通过酉演化对任意未知量子纯态制造其U-拷贝。该结果将原始不可克隆原理（U为单位算子的特例）推广到了所有酉变换情形。

Conclusion: 本文成功将量子不可克隆原理从原始的单位拷贝推广到了任意酉变换下的拷贝，为量子信息理论提供了更一般化的理论基础。

Abstract: It is known that the classical information like strings of bits can be copied. In 1982, Wootters and Zurek proposed the quantum no-cloning principle [1]. No-cloning principle says that it is impossible to make an identical copy of an arbitrary unknown quantum pure state by using unitary evolution. In this paper, we propose a general no-cloning principle. We call U|psi>, where U is any unitary operator, a U-copy of the state |psi>. The general no-cloning principle states that it is impossible to make a U-copy of an arbitrary unknown quantum pure state by using unitary evolution.

</details>


### [27] [Qutrit Clifford+T gates by two-body angular momentum couplings, rotations and one-axis-twistings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23007)
*F. E. S. Steinhoff*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了qutrit Clifford+T门集的角动量表示和实现方案，仅需旋转、单轴扭转（角动量算符的二次项）及线性角动量耦合即可实现全部门操作，并通过Jordan-Schwinger映射推广至玻色子模式，利用交叉Kerr相互作用实现任意Clifford+T门。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为qutrit量子计算中的Clifford+T门集提供一种物理上可实现的实验方案，降低实现难度。

Method: 利用角动量代数表示Clifford+T门，将局部门分解为旋转和单轴扭转操作（至多二次型），受控门仅需线性角动量耦合；通过Jordan-Schwinger映射转化为玻色子模式实现，并引入交叉Kerr相互作用。

Result: 完整qutrit Clifford+T门集可仅用两体角动量耦合、旋转和单轴扭转操作表达；玻色子实现方案相比已有方案减少了所需模式数；给出了制备纠缠态的简单方案。

Conclusion: 基于角动量的qutrit Clifford+T实现方案具有实验可行性，玻色子映射方案更具模式效率优势，适用于多种量子平台。

Abstract: We develop an angular momentum representation and implementation of the Clifford+T set of unitaries for qutrits. We show that local gates from this set can be realized by the sole use of suitable rotations and one-axis-twisting operations, which are at most quadratic in the angular momentum operators and thus can be experimentally realized in many quantum systems. Controlled rotations are shown to only require linear angular momentum couplings and, as a consequence, the full qutrit Clifford+T set is shown to be expressed solely in terms of two-body angular momentum couplings, rotations and one-axis-twisting operations. By employing the Jordan-Schwinger map, we show an analogous implementation in terms of bosonic modes, improving on the number of modes with regard to a previous scheme. Moreover, we employ the cross-Kerr interaction in order to obtain any qutrit Clifford+T gate for bosonic modes. We illustrate our findings with simple schemes for preparing entangled states of interest.

### [28] [Heralded Entanglement Transfer from Entangled Atomic Pair to Free Electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22974)
*Du Ran,Reuven Ianconescu,Shuai Liu,Ya-dong Li,Ji-Yuan Bai,Ze-Long He,Zhi-Cheng Shi,Yan Xia,Avraham Gover*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现自由电子之间的纠缠，推动量子电子光学的发展。

Method: 使用纠缠原子两级系统作为资源，通过局域电子-TLS相互作用将纠缠转移到能量边带梯子中的一对自由电子上；在受控旋转波近似下推导闭式约化态，并通过TLS heralding制备最大纠缠电子态。

Result: 推导了闭式约化态；TLS heralding可在二维单激发流形中制备最大纠缠电子态，纠缠度依赖于初始TLS资源纠缠；数值积分量化了失谐和脉冲整形的影响，识别了超出旋转波近似的主要修正。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了一条通往纠缠自由电子的heralded路径，将促进量子电子光学的进一步发展。

Abstract: We propose a protocol that transfers entanglement from an entangled atomic two-level-system (TLS) resource to a pair of free electrons in an energy-sideband ladder via local electron-TLS interactions. In a controlled rotating-wave regime, closed-form reduced states are derived. TLS heralding then prepares a maximally entangled electron state in a two-dimensional single-excitation manifold, with a simple dependence on the initial TLS resource entanglement. Numerical integration of the full bilinear Hamiltonian quantifies the impacts of detuning and pulse shaping and identifies the leading beyond-rotating-wave corrections. The results establish a heralded route to entangled free electrons and will facilitate further advances in quantum electron optics.

### [29] [Design Principles for Enhanced Quantum Transport with Site-Dependent Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23005)
*Maggie Lawrence,Elise Wang,Dvira Segal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究通过优化空间非均匀的退相干噪声来增强量子输运效率，发现与均匀退相干相比，位点优化的退相干能实现更高的输运效率，并伴随更强的稳态空间离域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究主要优化系统参数来提升环境噪声辅助量子输运，但忽略了环境噪声本身的空间结构。本文旨在通过允许位点依赖的退相干来直接优化环境噪声，从而更好地理解并控制开放系统中的量子输运。

Method: 采用Lindblad主方程框架，对斜坡势和随机无序势的一维晶格系统施加优化的局域退相干，分别考虑短程和长程相干隧穿，以稳态粒子流为优化目标，寻找最大化输运效率的退相干空间分布。

Result: 对于斜坡势，短程隧穿倾向于选择交替位点的退相干，长程隧穿则倾向于随注入点距离递增的退相干剖面。对于能量无序系统，强失谐位点需增强局域退相干以促进短程隧穿。所有情况下，位点优化退相干均优于均匀退相干，并伴有更强的稳态空间离域化。

Conclusion: 退相干通过局域展宽能级来克服失谐和相消干涉。空间结构化的环境噪声可作为控制开放系统中量子输运和态相干性的有效策略。

Abstract: Environmental noise can enhance transport, an effect known as environmental noise-assisted quantum transport. Most theoretical studies focus on optimizing system parameters under spatially uniform system-environment coupling. Here, instead, we optimize the environmental noise itself by allowing for site-dependent dephasing. We investigate steady-state transport in one-dimensional lattices with either ramped or disordered energy landscapes, considering both short- and long-range coherent tunneling. In the absence of environmental effects, in the thermodynamic limit these systems can exhibit localization, and thus suppressed transport, arising from destructive interference. Using a Lindblad master equation framework, we implement local dephasing optimized to maximize steady-state population flux. We find that for ramp potentials, short-range tunneling favors selective dephasing on alternating sites, whereas long-range tunneling benefits from a dephasing profile that increases with distance from the injection site. In energetically disordered systems, strongly detuned sites require enhanced local dephasing under short-range tunneling to facilitate transport. In all cases, we find that site-optimized dephasing allows higher transport efficiency than uniform dephasing, and it is accompanied by increased spatial delocalization of the steady state. Our results provide microscopic insight into the interplay between coherent dynamics and environmental noise. Dephasing broadens energy levels locally, helping to overcome detuning and destructive interference. More generally, we establish spatially-structured environmental noise as a strategy for controlling both quantum transport and state coherence in open systems.

</details>


### [30] [Accelerating quantum Gibbs sampling without quantum walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22996)
*Jiaqi Leng,Jiaqing Jiang,Lin Lin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无游走的量子算法，用于制备纯化的吉布斯态，在满足精确KMS细致平衡的一类量子吉布斯采样器上实现了谱隙依赖的二次改进。核心结构是将父哈密顿量分解为非交换一阶算子，将问题转化为奇异值滤波，并利用量子奇异值变换算法实现加速。此外，还引入了一种辅助耗散动力学，用于在亚稳态区域生成温启动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，将Szegedy量子游走的二次加速机制推广到量子吉布斯采样一直面临挑战，仅在特殊情况下可行。本文旨在克服这一限制，为更广泛的量子吉布斯采样器设计高效的量子算法。

Method: 1) 将父哈密顿量显式分解为非交换一阶算子；2) 将纯化吉布斯态制备转化为奇异值滤波问题；3) 应用量子奇异值变换算法实现谱隙依赖的二次改进；4) 基于相同分解引入辅助耗散动力学以生成温启动。

Result: 对于满足精确KMS细致平衡的一类量子吉布斯采样器，实现了谱隙依赖的二次改进。该框架适用范围超出Davies设定，涵盖了若干可高效实现的吉布斯采样器。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种系统性的无游走量子算法框架，通过非交换算子分解和量子奇异值变换，显著提升了纯化吉布斯态制备的效率，并拓展了适用采样器的范围。

Abstract: Szegedy's quantum walk gives a generic quadratic speedup for reversible classical Markov chains, but extending this mechanism to quantum Gibbs sampling has remained challenging beyond special cases. We present a walk-free quantum algorithm for preparing purified Gibbs states with a quadratic improvement in spectral-gap dependence for a broad class of quantum Gibbs samplers that satisfy exact Kubo-Martin-Schwinger detailed balance. Our main structural result is an explicit factorization of the corresponding parent Hamiltonian into noncommutative first-order operators. This turns purified Gibbs-state preparation into a singular-value filtering problem and enables a quantum singular value transformation algorithm with quadratically improved gap dependence under standard coherent-access assumptions. The framework applies to several efficiently implementable Gibbs samplers beyond the Davies setting. We also introduce an auxiliary dissipative dynamics based on the same factorization, which can be used to generate warm starts in the doubled Hilbert space in metastable regimes.

### [31] [Principles of relativistic quantum statistical thermodynamics: a class of exactly solvable models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23409)
*A. Yu. Zakharov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出将相互作用原子系统表示为原子子系统与辅助标量协变场的并集，该辅助场仅在非相对论近似下等价于给定的静态原子间势。辅助场是Klein-Gordon场的叠加，其参数与原子间势傅里叶变换的奇异点相关。建立了相对论性相互作用原子系统的哈密顿形式。精确计算相对论配分函数可归结为辅助场参数的重整化。经典相对论系统中场自由度导致总能量发散（紫外灾难类比），而辅助场的量子化可消除该发散。在相对论量子统计热力学框架内证明了相变的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多体原子系统中，原子间相互作用通常通过非相对论势函数描述，但严格的相对论处理要求将相互作用纳入协变场论框架。本文旨在建立一种严格形式，将静态原子间势嵌入相对论性场论表述，并探索由此带来的统计力学后果（如发散问题与相变）。

Method: 将原子系统（视为质点）与辅助标量场耦合，辅助场通过Klein-Gordon方程的线性组合构造，其参数由原子间势的傅里叶变换的极点（奇异点）确定。在相对论哈密顿形式中计算配分函数，通过场的正规化/重整化处理发散。最终对辅助场进行二次量子化以消除经典发散。

Result: 1) 原子间势可表示为Klein-Gordon场源的叠加；2) 相对论配分函数的精确计算简化为辅助场参数的重整化；3) 经典相对论场论中场自由度导致总能量紫外发散；4) 场的量子化可消除该发散；5) 在该相对论量子统计框架中预测了相变的存在。

Conclusion: 相对论性处理要求将原子间势替换为协变场，这自然引入了场自由度导致的发散问题，但量子化提供了自然的正则化机制。该框架不仅统一了相对论与统计力学，还预言了相变，为相对论多体理论提供了新的数学基础。

Abstract: A system of interacting atoms is represented as an union of two subsystems, one of which is the system of atoms, and the other is an auxiliary scalar covariant field, which is equivalent to a given static interatomic potential of general form only in the non-relativistic approximation. It is shown that the auxiliary field is a superposition of Klein-Gordon fields, the parameters of which are related to singular points of the Fourier transform of the corresponding interatomic potential. The general form of the relativistic Hamiltonian system of interacting atoms is established. It is shown that the exact calculation of the relativistic partition function of a system of interacting atoms, taking into account the field degrees of freedom, reduces to renormalizing the parameters of the auxiliary field. It is established that the field degrees of freedom lead to a divergence in the total energy of a classical relativistic system - an analogue of the ultraviolet catastrophe. Quantization of the auxiliary field eliminates this divergence. The existence of a phase transition within the framework of relativistic quantum statistical thermodynamics has been proven.

Abstract: In this work, we extend the class of previously introduced non-Euclidean neural quantum states (NQS) which consists only of Poincaré hyperbolic GRU, to new variants including Poincaré RNN as well as Lorentz RNN and Lorentz GRU. Here, in particular, using larger systems consisting of 100 spins, we found that all four hyperbolic RNN/GRU NQS variants always outperformed their respective Euclidean counterparts. Specifically, for all $J_2$ and $(J_2,J_3)$ couplings considered, including $J_2=0.0$, Lorentz RNN NQS and Poincaré RNN NQS always outperformd Euclidean RNN NQS, while Lorentz/Poincaré GRU NQS always outperformed Euclidean GRU NQS, with a single exception when $J_2=0.0$ for Poincaré GRU NQS. Furthermore, among the four hyperbolic NQS ansatzes, depending on the specific $J_2$ or $(J_2, J_3)$ couplings, on four out of eight experiment settings, Lorentz GRU and Poincaré GRU took turns to be the top performing variant among all Euclidean and hyperbolic NQS ansatzes considered, while Lorentz RNN, with up to three times fewer parameters, was capable of not only surpassing the Euclidean GRU eight out of eight times but also outperforming both Lorentz GRU and Poincaré GRU four out of eight times, to emerge as the best overall hyperbolic NQS ansatz.

### [33] [How fast can a quantum gate be? Exact speed limits from geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23031)
*Hunter Nelson,Edwin Barnes*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在哈密顿量谱宽有界的约束下，推导了适用于任意酉演化的通用紧致量子速度极限(QSL)，并将其应用于标准量子逻辑门（Hadamard、CNOT、Toffoli），发现不同门（即使具有相同纠缠能力）的QSL存在显著差异。通过空间曲线量子控制形式，将问题转化为受曲率约束的最短曲线问题，发现时间最优门映射为不同维度的螺旋线，并提出了瓶颈原则来解释最小门时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限能量资源下，量子演化速度存在根本性限制。现有量子速度极限大多基于量子态制定，但可扩展到演化算子本身，从而对量子计算机上逻辑门操作的实现速度施加基本限制。作者希望推导一个通用的、紧致的QSL，并理解不同量子门之间速度极限差异的几何本质。

Method: 首先在哈密顿量谱宽有界约束下，推导适用于任意酉演化的通用紧致QSL；然后将该结果应用于Hadamard、CNOT和Toffoli等标准量子门；最后利用空间曲线量子控制(SCQC)形式，将酉演化映射到欧氏空间中的空间曲线，将QSL问题转化为受曲率约束的最短路径问题，通过分析不同门对应的螺旋线维度来揭示门速度极限差异的几何原因。

Result: 得到了适用于任意酉演化的通用紧致QSL；发现不同量子门的QSL存在显著差异，即使是具有相同纠缠能力的门（如CNOT和某些门）也表现出不同的速度极限；时间最优门对应不同维度的螺旋线；提出了瓶颈原则：演化最慢的算子决定了最小门时间。

Conclusion: 本研究从几何角度深刻揭示了量子门速度极限的本质，为量子计算中门操作的优化提供了理论基础，特别是通过空间曲线形式将QSL问题转化为经典的最短路径问题，为设计时间最优量子门提供了新的几何视角。

Abstract: The speed of quantum evolution is limited under finite energy resources. While most quantum speed limits (QSLs) are formulated in terms of quantum states, they can be extended to the evolution operator itself, and thus impose fundamental limits on how quickly logical gate operations can be implemented on a quantum computer. Here, we derive a general, tight QSL that holds for any unitary evolution under the constraint that the spectral width of the Hamiltonian is bounded. We apply this result to obtain QSLs for several standard quantum gates, including Hadamard, CNOT, and Toffoli gates, finding that the QSL can vary significantly across different gates, including ones with the same entangling power. These findings can be understood geometrically using the Space Curve Quantum Control formalism, which maps unitary evolution to space curves in Euclidean space. In this formalism, the problem of finding QSLs is recast as the problem of finding minimal-length curves obeying a curvature bound. We find that time-optimal gates map to helices of varying dimensions, and that QSLs can be understood from the perspective of a bottleneck principle in which the operator that evolves the slowest governs the minimal gate time.

Abstract: In this paper, we study the non-Gaussianity of the eigenstates of the Pegg-Barnett phase observable. By computing the Wigner functions of the eigenstates, we confirm that they take negative values in specific regions of the phase space. The Pegg-Barnett phase-operator eigenstates lie on a finite-dimensional Hilbert space. Thus, we examine how their negativity volumes depend on the dimension of the Hilbert space. Moreover, we present a quantum-optical circuit that generates these eigenstates and identify single-photon detection as the origin of their non-Gaussianity. To investigate a more realistic experimental implementation, we introduce imperfect single-photon detectors with non-unit efficiency into the circuit and evaluate the dependence of the detection probability, the output-ideal fidelity, and the negativity volume of the approximate eigenstate output from the circuit on the detector efficiency. Finally, as a practical application, we consider a phase-estimation experiment of an arbitrary unknown state by injecting both the unknown state and a known Pegg-Barnett eigenstate into a 50-50 beam splitter and individually counting the numbers of photons emitted from its two output ports.

Result: 成功观测到高置信度的贝尔违例；在d=32时非定域性强度超过d=2的量子上界；验证了非定域性源自全体量子比特的集体贡献，而大多数二分对间关联仍保持贝尔局域性。

Conclusion: 当前量子处理器能够探索量子力学在先前不可达区域的基本预言，同时这类量子效应可用于基准测试量子处理器的性能。

Abstract: Combining recent advances in superconducting quantum hardware, we explore quantum correlations in a previously inaccessible regime by observing \emph{simultaneously} high-dimensional and many-body Bell non-locality. We report a high-confidence Bell violation in the correlations between two $d=64$-dimensional systems encoded in twelve qubits. For system sizes up to $d=32$, the strength of the observed nonlocal correlations exceeds the quantum upper bound for $d=2$ systems, providing direct evidence of high-dimensional nonlocality. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the observed violation is genuinely collective: all qubits contribute to the nonlocal correlations, while most pairwise correlations across the bipartition remain Bell-local. Our work illustrates how present-day quantum processors enable the exploration of fundamental predictions of quantum mechanics in previously inaccessible regimes and, in turn, how fundamental quantum effects can be used to benchmark their performance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了基于对易图着色技术的分组排序策略，将哈密顿项划分为组内互相对易的子集；同时对比了若干基线排序策略，并在1D和2D海森堡模型上计算了真实的特罗特误差。

Abstract: Trotterization is a technique that allows one to approximate a time evolution of a Hamiltonian by repeatedly evolving the individual terms of the Hamiltonian one-at-a-time for small time durations. Bounds on the error of this approximation exist; however, they are typically loose and moreover, it is known that the true error can be greatly influenced by the order in which the terms of the Hamiltonian are evolved. In this work, we consider various ordering strategies that exploit the commutation structure of the Hamiltonian, in addition to a few other baseline ordering strategies. These commutation-based strategies involve dividing the terms of the Hamiltonian into groups where all the terms within each group commute with one another. These groupings can be obtained by using graph coloring techniques on what we call the "commutation graph" of the Hamiltonian. We prove various results regarding the structure and properties of such commutation graphs for certain classes of Hamiltonians. We also empirically calculate the (true) Trotter error using these ordering strategies on various 1D and 2D Heisenberg-style systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先定义测量概率的速度为测量结果惊奇度的平均变化率，证明该速度受限于测量概率中的量子涨落。通过选择最优局域投影测量，该量子速度极限可作为两体量子关联的判据。进一步推导从初始测量概率到目标测量概率的最小转换时间，并将结果应用于分析生成局域非热性所需量子不确定性的代价。

Result: 测量概率的速度存在一个由量子涨落决定的量子速度极限；该极限可通过优化局域投影测量来检测两体量子关联；得到了测量概率转换的最小时间下限，并量化了生成局域非热性所需的量子不确定性代价。

Conclusion: 本文建立了测量概率转换过程中的时间-能量-量子资源之间的基本限制关系，为量子信息处理中的资源理论提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Any protocol to process quantum information has to conclude with a measurement, aimed at producing a specific set of probabilities of measurement outcomes. In this work, we investigate the time, energy and importantly the genuine quantum resources necessary for transforming a set of measurement probabilities generated by a positive-operator-valued measure (POVM), to a target set of measurement probabilities. To this end, we first show that the speed of measurement probabilities, defined as the average rate of the surprisal of measurement outcomes, is constrained by the genuine quantum fluctuations contained in the measurement probabilities. Interestingly, this quantum speed limit can act as a witness for bipartite quantum correlations by selecting an optimal local projective measurement. Furthermore, we obtain a minimum time to transform an initial measurement probabilities to a target measurement probabilities, and apply this result to analyzing the cost of generating a local athermality in terms of genuine quantum uncertainty.

### [39] [Quantum criticality from spectral collapse in the two-photon Rabi model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23164)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析各向异性双光子量子Rabi模型的能谱结构，研究同一宇称内激发能隙的闭合行为（临界指数zν=1/2），并利用量子Fisher信息和Kibble-Zurek动力学等工具表征平衡与非平衡性质。

Abstract: Spectral collapse in the two-photon quantum Rabi model (tpQRM) has long been regarded as incompatible with quantum criticality due to the absence of a vanishing excitation gap. We show that, in the anisotropic tpQRM, spectral collapse constitutes a genuine continuous quantum phase transition governed by a single soft mode. The excitation gap within the same parity closes as $ε_{sp} \sim |g - g_c|^{zν}$ with $zν= 1/2$, placing the system in the same universality class as the standard QRM, while the gap between different parities reflects symmetry-induced level splitting rather than a critical excitation. This soft mode defines a unique energy scale that controls both equilibrium and nonequilibrium properties, including macroscopic observables, quantum Fisher information, and Kibble-Zurek dynamics. These results establish spectral collapse as an experimentally accessible realization of quantum criticality in a few-body system and demonstrate that universality is fully determined by the soft-mode structure rather than by microscopic details.

Method: 提出"峰谷（PV） fragmentation"机制：通过设计简单的局域规则，使计算基下自旋态可被一组涌现的好量子数标记，这些量子数对应于几何表征中交替峰谷的高度和深度。

Abstract: Ergodicity breaking in isolated systems has emerged as an important frontier in the study of quantum many-body physics. While generic Hamiltonians are expected to obey the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH), recent studies on Hilbert space fragmentation (HSF) have revealed possible robust nonthermal behavior even in disorder-free systems. Although numerous models exhibiting strong HSF are already known, existing analyses are typically model dependent, and a general organizing principle remains elusive. In this work, we introduce a simple mechanism for achieving strong HSF in one-dimensional integer spin chains, which we term "peak-valley (PV) fragmentation". The key idea is to devise a simple local rule which ensures the spin states in the computational basis can be labeled by a set of emergent good quantum numbers corresponding to the heights and depths of alternating peaks and valleys in a geometrical representation. We demonstrate that some known examples of strong HSF models, as well as their variants which break the HSF property, can be understood within the framework of PV fragmentation. Our approach also enables systematic construction of new fragmented models in higher-spin systems, and allows us to identify higher-order HSF models.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The Barnett effect is usually understood through an effective magnetic field generated by mechanical rotation, while its reciprocal Einstein--de Haas effect describes the transfer of spin angular momentum to mechanical motion. We show that this effective-field picture changes qualitatively once the mechanical degree of freedom itself is quantized. To demonstrate this, we introduce an exactly solvable minimal spin-rotor model in which a spin-$1/2$ is coupled to a quantum rotor. In a fixed angular-momentum sector, the model reproduces the conventional Barnett splitting and remains formally equivalent to a Zeeman problem. For a superposition of rotor sectors, however, the Barnett field becomes operator-valued and the resulting dynamics generates coherent spin-rotor entanglement. This is directly visible in the reduced spin purity, rotor coherence, and entanglement entropy. Our results identify a minimal quantum setting in which the Barnett effective-field picture departs from its classical form and acquires a reciprocal manifestation through spin-dependent rotor coherence.

### [44] [Introducing the Correlation Concentration Ratio (CCR): Quantitative Framework for Comparing Quantum Cluster States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23258)
*Amin Ahadi,Saman Sarshar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了不同拓扑结构的四模连续变量簇态，利用辛表示和协方差矩阵系统建模了线性、方形和T形拓扑的簇态生成过程。结果表明簇图结构直接反映在正交关联模式中，并引入了一个名为CCR（相关集中比）的度量指标，用于量化有效相关在图像边缘上的集中程度，从而为基于测量的量子计算架构中簇图拓扑的选择和优化提供工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，利用辛表示和协方差矩阵对线性、方形和T形三种拓扑的四模连续变量簇态生成过程进行建模；引入CCR（Correlation Concentration Ratio）指标，量化有效相关在图像边缘上的集中程度。

Result: 簇图结构直接反映在正交关联模式中，理论零化关系在最终协方差矩阵中得到复现；增大压缩参数可增强目标关联并抑制反压缩带来的不需要分量；线性与方形拓扑中协方差矩阵非对角元显著增大，T形拓扑中呈现更强的中心关联（类似连续变量领域GHZ行为）。CCR指标能够有效区分不同拓扑的结构性差异。

Abstract: In this paper, numerical simulations of four-mode continuous-variable cluster states with different topologies in the framework of measurement-based quantum computation are presented. By utilizing the symplectic representation and covariance matrix, the process of generating cluster states with linear, square, and T-shaped topologies has been systematically modeled. The simulation results show that the cluster graph structure is directly reflected in the pattern of quadrature correlations; in other words, the theoretical nullifier relations of the cluster states are reproduced in the final covariance matrices. Increasing the squeezing parameter leads to the strengthening of the target correlations and the suppression of unwanted components arising from anti-squeezing; such that the off-diagonal elements of the covariance matrix in the linear and square topologies increase to significant values, and in the T-shaped topology a stronger central correlation (similar to GHZ-like behavior in the continuous-variable domain) is observed. In order to quantitatively analyze these structural differences, a metric titled CCR (Correlation Concentration Ratio) is introduced that quantifies the concentration of effective correlations on the graph edges relative to the total correlations of the system. This index enables direct comparison of different topologies from the perspective of structural entanglement distribution and provides a framework for evaluating the efficiency of cluster graphs in MBQC architectures. The results show that CCR can be used as a practical tool for designing and selecting optimal topologies in larger clusters and more complex structures.

Motivation: 探索双层狄拉克材料中准粒子间的动量空间纠缠机制，理解腔耦合下自能重整化对纠缠熵的影响，以及实现贝尔态的可能性。

Result: 在微扰可控区域内熵保持较小；唯象自能修飾驱动交叉行为，使纠缠熵显著增强；只有当准粒子相干时间超过层间光子传播时间时才能获得稳态纠缠；最大熵区域可能是实现贝尔态的有效方法。

Conclusion: 自能重整化、虚粒子交换与旋量几何的协同效应决定了狄拉克材料中动量空间纠缠的演化，最大纠缠态有望用于量子信息处理。

Abstract: We investigate the momentum-space entanglement between two Dirac quasiparticles in a double-layer honeycomb lattice coupled via a planar electromagnetic cavity. We model the low-energy excitations as massive Dirac fermions in $(1+2)$ dimensions and derive the Bethe-Salpeter equation using the ladder approximation. We use a Born-level approximation around a free two-body quasiparticle state, where the interaction is mediated by the cavity photon propagator. From the reduced sublattice density matrix, we compute a momentum-resolved von Neumann entropy. Within the perturbatively controlled regime, the entropy remains small, while phenomenological self-energy dressing drives a crossover to strong enhancement of the entanglement entropy. Stationary entanglement is obtained only when the quasiparticle coherence time exceeds the photon propagation time between the layers. The maximum-entropy regime appears to be a viable method for achieving Bell-like states. These results demonstrate how self-energy renormalization, virtual particle exchange, and spinor geometry combine to reshape the entanglement landscape of Dirac materials.

### [46] [Quantum Sufficiency for Self-Adjoint Statistical Models via Likelihood-Type Operators on Real $*$-Subalgebras and Real Jordan Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23292)
*Koichi Yamagata*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套基于实*-子代数和实Jordan代数的量子充分性理论，统一处理了普通量子统计模型和局部量子统计结构，揭示了实Jordan结构是量子理论统计方面的自然框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子充分性理论基于态族、复完全正粗粒化和忠实参考态的Radon-Nikodym余环，无法统一处理普通量子统计模型和局部量子统计结构。本文旨在建立一个更广泛的框架，使平方根似然比和对称对数导数等自伴算子自然出现，并统一处理退化的参考态。

Method: 引入充分实正映射的概念，将充分复*-子代数、充分实*-子代数和充分实Jordan代数分别对应到复完全正映射、实完全正映射和实正映射。利用似然比集和ρ-模不变性刻画最小充分实*-子代数，并证明由似然比集与投影参考态生成的实Jordan代数是最小充分实Jordan代数。还建立了Koashi-Imoto型分解。

Result: 提出了充分实正映射的概念，建立了三种充分性结构的对应关系；用似然比集和ρ-模不变性刻画了最小充分实*-子代数；证明似然比集与投影参考态生成的实Jordan代数是最小充分实Jordan代数；得到了充分实*-子代数和充分实Jordan代数的Koashi-Imoto型分解。

Conclusion: 实Jordan结构为量子理论的统计方面提供了超越传统复*-代数框架的自然框架，能够统一处理普通统计模型和局部统计结构，并分离了充分性的似然比方面和真正的量子模方面。

Abstract: We develop a theory of quantum sufficiency on real *-subalgebras and real Jordan algebras. In contrast to the conventional formulation, which is based on families of states, complex completely positive coarse-grainings, and Radon-Nikodym cocycles associated with faithful reference states, our framework allows models consisting of general self-adjoint operators, including derivatives of states. Within this framework, square-root likelihood ratios and symmetric logarithmic derivatives arise naturally as fundamental self-adjoint likelihood-type objects. This makes it possible to treat ordinary quantum statistical models and local quantum statistical structures within a unified setting.
  We introduce sufficient real positive maps and show that sufficient complex *-subalgebras, sufficient real *-subalgebras, and sufficient real Jordan algebras correspond respectively to complex completely positive maps, real completely positive maps, and real positive maps. We characterize minimal sufficient real *-subalgebras by the likelihood-ratio set together with rho-modular invariance, and show that the real Jordan algebra generated by the likelihood-ratio set and the projected reference state is the minimal sufficient real Jordan algebra. We also obtain Koashi-Imoto type decompositions for sufficient real *-subalgebras and sufficient real Jordan algebras. Our formulation admits degenerate reference states and separates the likelihood-ratio aspect of sufficiency from its genuinely quantum modular aspect. These results suggest that real Jordan structure provides a natural framework for the statistical aspect of quantum theory beyond the conventional complex *-algebraic setting.

### [48] [Intrinsic Pointer Basis and Irreversible Classicality from Coherence Contraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23304)
*José J. Gil*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于密度算子本征分解的经典性涌现理论，通过定义内禀参考基（IRB）将密度算子分解为对角人口部分和实反对称相干部分，证明了在马尔可夫开放系统动力学中二次相干泛函是Lyapunov泛函，并由此导出了规范化的凝聚指数作为可操作的经典性判据，以及可通过最慢退相速率计算的经典化时间。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过固定物理共轭K（由测量约定、系统对称性或久期近似决定）定义内禀参考基（IRB），对角化态的实对称部分；将密度算子分解为对角人口和实反对称相干部分；证明在IRB对角Lindblad算子的马尔可夫开放系统动力学下，二次相干泛函是Lyapunov泛函；定义归一化凝聚指数作为可操作的经典性判据。

Conclusion: 该方法补充了环境诱导超选择理论，适用于任何存在粗粒化约化描述的场景，无需知道微观系统-环境耦合的具体形式，且可通过标准干涉设备直接检验经典性判据。

Abstract: The irreversible emergence of classical behavior from a reduced quantum description via a canonical intrinsic decomposition of the density operator is analyzed. In the intrinsic reference basis (IRB), defined for a fixed physical conjugation K (determined by measurement convention, system symmetry, or secular approximation) by diagonalizing the real symmetric part of the state, the density operator separates into a diagonal population sector and a real antisymmetric coherence sector. For the class of Markovian open-system dynamics whose Lindblad operators are diagonal in the IRB, we prove that the quadratic coherence functional is a Lyapunov functional under pure-dephasing or interaction-picture evolution, with each intrinsic coherence component decaying exponentially at a computable rate. This yields a canonical state-dependent operational classicality criterion via the normalized cohesion index, an explicit logarithmic classicalization time controlled by the slowest dephasing rate, and a demonstration that the IRB projectors emerge as dynamically stable pointer sectors under IRB-selective evolution. Suppression of intrinsic coherences is exactly equivalent to suppression of fringe visibility in the corresponding interferometric sector; for a balanced two-path setup the cohesion index coincides with the fringe visibility, making the classicality criterion directly testable with standard interferometric equipment. The approach complements environment-induced einselection: it is applicable whenever a coarse-grained reduced description is available, independently of whether the microscopic system-environment coupling is known.

### [49] [Complementarity between bosonic and fermionic many-body interferences with partially distinguishable particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23316)
*Marco Robbio,Michael G. Jabbour,Nicolas J. Cerf*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了玻色子和费米子在部分可区分（如偏振或时间延迟差异）情况下，仍满足干涉互补性关系，该关系通过永久式与行列式的张量恒等式表达，并导出粒子数分布相关矩阵的求和规则，进而约束量子计量学中相位估计的量子Fisher信息，揭示了可区分性对玻色子和费米子灵敏度相反的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究已从数学上刻画了玻色子和费米子在完全不可区分时的干涉互补性（arXiv:2312.17709），但实际实验中粒子往往部分可区分（如偏振、时间延迟差异），因此需要探究该互补性在部分可区分条件下是否依然成立。

Method: 通过建立部分可区分情形下玻色子和费米子多粒子干涉的数学关系，推导出将三阶张量的永久式与行列式联系的新恒等式；进而分析干涉仪输出端粒子数分布的相关矩阵，导出玻色子与费米子相关矩阵之和等于两倍经典粒子相关矩阵的求和规则。

Result: 1) 部分可区分情形下玻色-费米干涉互补性仍然成立；2) 得到三阶张量永久式与行列式的新数学恒等式；3) 玻色子和费米子输出粒子数分布的相关矩阵满足简单求和规则；4) 该求和规则约束了相位估计中可达的量子Fisher信息，表现为：更高不可区分性增强玻色子灵敏度，而降低不可区分性有利于费米子方案。

Conclusion: 该研究将玻色-费米干涉互补性从完全不可区分推广到部分可区分情形，为量子计量学中利用粒子统计与区分性调控灵敏度提供了理论基础，并揭示了玻色子和费米子在相位估计中关于可区分性的非对称权衡关系。

Abstract: It is well known that bosons and fermions exhibit opposite behaviors when experiencing interference, in the sense that bosons have a tendency to bunch whereas fermions have a tendency to antibunch. Recently, this complementarity was mathematically characterized in [arXiv:2312.17709] by means of an identity relating the transition probabilities of both types of particles in a linear interferometer. Here, we show that such a complementarity still holds even when particles become partially distinguishable, for example, when they have slightly different polarizations or time delays. Namely, we establish a relation that combines bosonic and fermionic multiparticle interferences in an arbitrary linear interferometer, in the presence of partial distinguishability. Incidentally, this also provides a new mathematical identity relating the permanent and determinant of tensors of order 3. Importantly, this complementarity has direct operational consequences in quantum metrology. Indeed, we show that the correlation matrices for bosonic and fermionic particle number distributions at the output of the interferometer obey a simple sum rule: their sum equals twice the correlation matrix for classical particles. This, in turn, constraints the achievable quantum Fisher information in phase-estimation protocols, highlighting a trade-off whereby greater indistinguishability enhances bosonic sensitivity whereas reduced indistinguishability can benefit fermionic schemes.

Exploiting that quantum measurements are projections, we propose a model reduction approach and show that simulations can be conducted in a lower-dimensional space. The dressed states comprising the latter give their place to a self-consistent spontaneous dressed-state polarization as the driving strength is lowered. The associated evolution proves anew highly contextual, underpinned by a persistent production of coherent-state superpositions for a particular setting of the monitoring device. Finally, when bistability is absent, we employ the photoelectron `atomic' emission statistics as a diagnostic tool of the cavity field fluctuations.

Abstract: We have developed a non-unitary extension of Grover's search algorithm by changing the hidden geometry of Hilbert space carried by diffusion operator. Our algorithm finds the solution for search problem by performing a unique bigger rotation rather than small rotations in order polynomial times in the size $N$ of search space. We analyze the complexity of implementing the non-unitary operation and we observed that the price paid by performing this rotation is due the normalization. In Kraus operator approach we need $O(N)$ repetition of the algorithm to have a chance of measuring a solution in a post-selection, this is no better than the classical solution. However, the quantum singular value transform in addition with block encoding and Chebyshev polynomial approximation, we got complexity $O(\sqrt{N})$ and reach the Grover's bound with an extra resource of one single qubit, compared with the standard Grover's algorithm.

### [53] [From Independent to Joint: Enhancing Quantum Phase and Correlation Factor Estimation by Squeezed Reservoir Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23476)
*Cai-Hong Liao,Yan-Ling Li,Long Huang,Xing Xiao*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了利用关联压缩热库和压缩相位来增强量子参数估计精度，推导了相位匹配条件以最大化量子Fisher信息和最小化联合估计方差，证明在优化压缩相位条件下联合估计能节约量子资源并保持高精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子参数估计的高精度对量子计量学至关重要，尽管库工程能通过调控系统-环境相互作用来改善估计精度，但压缩相位以及顺序利用同一压缩库产生的关联性在参数估计中的作用尚未被充分探索。

Method: 采用关联压缩热库（correlated squeezed-thermal reservoir），分别独立和同时估计相位参数φ和关联因子μ；通过量子Fisher信息（QFI）分析推导近最优相位匹配条件，以最大化F_φ和F_μ并最小化联合估计总方差Δ_sim；使用方差比R评估联合估计的性能。

Result: 发现压缩相位Φ对实现量子增强精度至关重要，且最优相位匹配条件强烈依赖于μ；联合估计方差主要由F_φ主导；在优化F_φ的相位匹配条件下，尽管参数存在固有不相容性，联合估计仍能节约量子资源并保持高精度。

Conclusion: 这些发现为利用库工程策略实现高精度量子传感与信息处理提供了实用的见解。

Abstract: High-precision quantum parameter estimation is fundamental to the advancement of quantum metrology. Although reservoir engineering provides a powerful approach to improve estimation by tailoring system-environment interactions, the role of the squeezing phase and correlations arising from the sequential utilization of the same squeezed reservoir remains inadequately explored. In this work, we employ a correlated squeezed-thermal reservoir to enhance the precision of estimating the phase parameter $φ$ and the correlation factor $μ$, both individually and simultaneously. We show that the squeezing phase $Φ$ is crucial for achieving quantum-enhanced precision, with optimal phase-matching conditions that depend strongly on $μ$. Specifically, we derive the near-optimal phase-matching relations aimed at maximizing the quantum Fisher information (QFI) for both $φ$ and $μ$, as well as minimizing the total variance $Δ_{\rm sim}$ in joint estimation. Furthermore, we show that the joint estimation variance is dominated by $F_φ$, which motivates our search for the phase-matching conditions that minimize $Δ_{\text{sim}}$. Through the ratio $R$ of variances, we demonstrate that joint estimation conserves quantum resources and maintains high precision when the squeezing phase is optimized for $F_φ$, despite the inherent incompatibility of the parameters. These findings provide practical insights into reservoir engineering strategies for high-precision quantum sensing and information processing.

### [54] [Efficient Quantum Fully Homomorphic Encryption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23490)
*Fengxia Liu,Zixian Gong,Kun Tian,Yi Zhang,Zhiming Zheng,Maozhi Xu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种统一框架，通过整合模块化算术程序(MAP)、花园软管模型和基于测量的量子计算(MBQC)，实现了量子全同态加密(QFHE)的指数级效率提升。核心创新是设计了针对LWE解密代数结构的新型MAP，将量子 gadget 所需的EPR对从O(λ^{2.58})降至O(λ log² λ)，实际改进因子达2^{15}至2^{18}倍。方案支持全经典客户端，仅依赖经典LWE假设，避免了循环安全或量子困难性假设。

  <summary>Details</summary>
